leader.\n    65→     *\n    66→     * action: respond to heartbeats with REBALANCE_IN_PROGRESS\n    67→     *         respond to offset commits with REBALANCE_IN_PROGRESS\n    68→     *         park STABLE\n    71→     *             join group from new member or existing member with updated metadata => PREPARING_REBALANCE\n    72→     *             leave group from existing member => \"text\": \"The Kafka consumer group coordinator's state machine is implemented across multiple Java files in the group-coordinator module. The core state machine is defined in ClassicGroupState.java (apache/kafka), which is an enum representing five states: EMPTY, PREPARING_REBALANCE, COMPLETING_REBALANCE, STABLE, and DEAD. These states correspond to phases of the consumer group rebalancing protocol: EMPTY and PREPARING_REBALANCE represent the join phase where members join the group; COMPLETING_REBALANCE represents the sync phase where the leader assigns partitions and members synchronize; STABLE represents normal operation; and DEAD represents group cleanup.\\n\\nThe ClassicGroup.java file (apache/kafka) contains the state machine implementation logic, including the transitionTo() method (line 991) which enforces valid state transitions, and the assertValidTransition() method (line 1464) which validates transitions against the validPreviousStates() set defined in ClassicGroupState. Each state has pre-defined valid previous states: EMPTY can follow PREPARING_REBALANCE; PREPARING_REBALANCE can follow STABLE, COMPLETING_REBALANCE, or EMPTY; COMPLETING_REBALANCE follows PREPARING_REBALANCE; and STABLE follows COMPLETING_REBALANCE. The class maintains state tracking with private fields for current state, previous state, and state timestamps.\\n\\nThe state machine transitions are driven by request handling in GroupMetadataManager.java. The maybePrepareRebalanceOrCompleteJoin() method initiates the join phase by transitioning to PREPARING_REBALANCE, while completeClassicGroupJoin() (triggered when all members have joined) transitions to COMPLETING_REBALANCE for the sync phase. These methods coordinate with member tracking through ClassicGroupMember.java, which manages individual member state during the rebalancing process.\\n\\nModern consumer group coordination (KIP-848 protocol) is implemented in ConsumerGroup.java with its own ConsumerGroupState enum containing states EMPTY, ASSIGNING, RECONCILING, and STABLE. This modern state machine uses a different approach with timeline-backed states and epoch-based coordination, coordinated through the maybeUpdateGroupState() method which dynamically determines state based on member epochs and reconciliation status.\\n\\nThe state machine integrates with the broader group coordination through GroupCoordinator.java, which exposes joinGroup() and syncGroup() methods that trigger state transitions. \"The Kafka consumer group coordinator's state machine is implemented across multiple Java files in the group-coordinator module. The core state machine is defined in ClassicGroupState.java (apache/kafka), which is an enum representing five states: EMPTY, PREPARING_REBALANCE, COMPLETING_REBALANCE, STABLE, and DEAD. These states correspond to phases of the consumer group rebalancing protocol: EMPTY and PREPARING_REBALANCE represent the join phase where members join the group; COMPLETING_REBALANCE represents the sync phase where the leader assigns partitions and members synchronize; STABLE represents normal operation; and DEAD represents group cleanup.\\n\\nThe ClassicGroup.java file (apache/kafka) contains the state machine implementation logic, including the transitionTo() method (line 991) which enforces valid state transitions, and the assertValidTransition() method (line 1464) which validates transitions against the validPreviousStates() set defined in ClassicGroupState. Each state has pre-defined valid previous states: EMPTY can follow PREPARING_REBALANCE; PREPARING_REBALANCE can follow STABLE, COMPLETING_REBALANCE, or EMPTY; COMPLETING_REBALANCE follows PREPARING_REBALANCE; and STABLE follows COMPLETING_REBALANCE. The class maintains state tracking with private fields for current state, previous state, and state timestamps.\\n\\nThe state machine transitions are driven by request handling in GroupMetadataManager.java. The maybePrepareRebalanceOrCompleteJoin() method initiates the join phase by transitioning to PREPARING_REBALANCE, while completeClassicGroupJoin() (triggered when all members have joined) transitions to COMPLETING_REBALANCE for the sync phase. These methods coordinate with member tracking through ClassicGroupMember.java, which manages individual member state during the rebalancing process.\\n\\nModern consumer group coordination (KIP-848 protocol) is implemented in ConsumerGroup.java with its own ConsumerGroupState enum containing states EMPTY, ASSIGNING, RECONCILING, and STABLE.
